  126. To see what I use each of these brushes for read my blog post:<br />[...]<br /><br />I had high hopes for these but I do realize they are an extremely low cost set so they are not perfect but they are definitely worth the money. The face brushes don't pick up product well, the type of fibers they used are too slippery. I was able to get a light application of blush so that's nice, especially if you tend to be heavy handed. It wouldn't really pick up loose powder at all. I'm going to try spraying the ends with MAC Fix+ or the similar one by elf and see if I have better luck. I think these would be good for applying a light dusting of shimmer highlight to your cheekbones. None of the brushes are great for applying eyeshadow or blending, they are more the type for applying cream eyeshadow or highlight. You might be able to use the flat eyeshadow brushes for packing on color, if it is a high pigmented shadow. They would work great wet to get a nice defined edge. These type of stiff flat brushes are great for concealer, primer, cream products, lipstick, gel liner, etc. so you will have a whole array of brushes to fill out your brush collection for that stuff but you will probably need to pick up a few better eyeshadow brushes, especially for blending, as there is nothing in here that works for that. The little square brush is for tight lining your lashes, where you pack on gel eyeliner right into your lash line for dark, luscious lashes. All in all, I am glad I bought these, it is a great starter set or to fill out your collection but you will need to supplement a few other brushes to be really happy with your makeup application. I have 6 different brush sets and I recommend first picking up the Real Techniques Core Collection for face brushes and the Starter set for the eyeshadow brushes. The Elf Studio Brushes are amazing and you can often get them for 50% off, making them $1.50 a brush. If you are like me and you want multiples of every brush this is a great set for that but I just wish it had some softer fluffier eye brushes for blending and eyeshadow. Still an amazing deal and so cute with the pink tips!<br /><br />**EDIT** I decided to try these brushes exclusively as if they were my only brushes and I was able to improvise and get a nice application of makeup. Be open minded and you can use some brushes for other uses than they are intended, for example I packed on a crease color with a small \\"eyeshadow brush\\" and blended it out gently with the fan brush. Be gentle and build up color, yes the small brushes are fairly stiff but if you use a light hand they will work very well. Foundation brushes work great for sweeping away fallout and also perfectly blending out an eyeshadow wing if you do a smoky eye. ;) Also I put a little hair gel on my fan brush while it was wet to make it stiffer and now it is much better for sweeping away fallout. Spraying a little Fix+ works very well with these brushes to make a precise application of color. This set is an excellent value and it may not be my preferred brushes but not everyone wants to spend a lot of $$$ on this kind of stuff. I'm upping my rating to 5 stars because if you are willing to give these a chance and think a little outside the box I think you will be happy with these. Also if the ferrel comes off the handle big deal, just paint on a little nail polish & push those suckers back on, they will stay on after that.hat but I just wish it had some softer fluffier eye brushes for blending and eyeshadow. Still an amazing deal and so cute with the pink tips!<br /><br />**EDIT** I decided to try these brushes exclusively as if they were my only brushes and I was able to improvise and get a nice application of makeup. However, I was pleasantly surprised.<br /><br />The brushes are really nicely colored, and have a good aesthetic quality to them if you like loads of pink. The color is actually even a tad brighter in person.<br /><br />I am giving you this review from the perspective of a professional makeup artist.<br />My overall view of the product is that it can be a good starting brush set for the young makeup enthusiast who may just be learning and building their makeup kit. It is also a good product to have for people who just like to collect different kinds of brushes. This is not a &#34;complete&#34; brush set. Brushes will need to be added to this. I repeat, THIS IS NOT A STAND ALONE BRUSH SET FOR PROFESSIONALS. Great for young/new makeup enthusiasts/brush collectors.<br /><br />[MORE IN DEPTH REVIEW BELOW]<br /><br />The brush roll is nice! The color is nice, the brush slots do their job, & I didn't have any problem with a smell as others have said. It smelled like a new brush roll for a bit, then it faded. Just like a new car smell fades over time. I've not had a single issue with the brush roll at all. If I was being extremely picky, I might say that I was just wishing it could be more of a brush belt, but that's not what the product is advertised as. It's a brush roll, so I can't complain there.<br />The large powder brush and the smaller blush/powder brush work well for the application of those products. The large fan brush works well for dusting off excess powders and moderately well for blending out powder blushes/contour along with applying highlight down the nose and on the cheeks. There are a couple smaller brushes that I've used as lip brushes that work well for that.<br />The foundation brush is okay for putting the product on the face. I find it's best used to help blend out when I do liquid highlightsand contours. The stippling brush is not nearly dense enough and the bristles are just too long and &#34;loose&#34; to have any practical use. The eyeshadow brushes didn't impress me either. They weren't fantastic with picking up or packing shadows, and this set doesn't come with any type of fluffy blending brush. The eyeliner brush didn't work too well for me as it doesn't seem to hold its shape very well. It gets stray hairs that can get product all over the lid.<br />The little tools for the eyebrows and lashes work well. You can't really go wrong with those.<br /><br />For the price you pay, these are GREAT products, but that doesn't mean that they're GREAT brushes.
